32. 收缩自编码器 (CAE) 公式

  • 链接：https://apxml.com/zh/courses/autoencoders-representation-learning/chapter-3-regularized-autoencoders/contractive-autoencoders-formulation
  • 来源：bing
  • 摘要：收缩自编码器和去噪自编码器都旨在学习对输入变化不太敏感的表示。 然而，它们实现此目标的方式不同： DAEs: 隐式地 学习鲁棒性，通过训练模型从随机损坏的版本重建原始输入。 模型必须学习足够稳定 …
  • 易漏细节梳理：

收缩自编码器旨在学习对输入变化不太敏感的表示，通过惩罚编码器输出对输入的无穷小变化的敏感性来实现这一目标。雅可比矩阵衡量编码器输出对输入的偏导数，而收缩惩罚项与雅可比矩阵的平方弗罗贝尼乌斯范数成比例。损失函数是重建损失与收缩惩罚项的和。较大的λ会强制更强的收缩，但可能会影响重建质量。收缩自编码器促使编码器在训练数据点附近具有收缩性，促使编码器局部学习数据流形的切空间。现代深度学习框架可以高效地计算这种惩罚。此外，收缩自编码器和去噪自编码器都旨在学习对输入变化不太敏感的表示，但收缩自编码器通过添加惩罚项直接最小化所学特征相对于输入扰动的敏感性，而去噪自编码器通过训练模型从随机损坏的版本重建原始输入来实现鲁棒性。选择收缩自编码器或去噪自编码器取决于具体任务和数据中预期变化的性质。

  • 关键点（易漏细节）：
  • 收缩自编码器旨在学习对输入变化不太敏感的表示。
  • 收缩自编码器通过惩罚编码器输出对输入的无穷小变化的敏感性来实现这一目标。
  • 雅可比矩阵衡量编码器输出对输入的偏导数。
  • 收缩惩罚项与雅可比矩阵的平方弗罗贝尼乌斯范数成比例。
  • 损失函数是重建损失与收缩惩罚项的和。
  • 较大的λ会强制更强的收缩，但可能会影响重建质量。
  • 收缩自编码器促使编码器在训练数据点附近具有收缩性。
  • 收缩映射促使编码器局部学习数据流形的切空间。
  • 现代深度学习框架可以高效地计算这种惩罚。
  • 收缩自编码器和去噪自编码器都旨在学习对输入变化不太敏感的表示。
  • 收缩自编码器通过添加惩罚项直接最小化所学特征相对于输入扰动的敏感性。
  • 去噪自编码器通过训练模型从随机损坏的版本重建原始输入来实现鲁棒性。
  • 选择收缩自编码器或去噪自编码器取决于具体任务和数据中预期变化的性质。

收缩自编码器（CAEs）开发对微小输入变化具有鲁棒性的表示。这些模型明确旨在使所学特征映射（由编码器函数 f ( x ) f(x) f ( x ) 表示）对输入数据 x x x 的微小变化不敏感。这与其他自编码器类型不同，例如稀疏自编码器侧重于通过将不重要的潜在单元置零来寻找简洁表示，而去噪自编码器则通过从损坏版本重建数据来学习。 核心思想是 收缩 。我们希望自编码器学习一种映射，使得输入空间中的微小变化对应于潜在特征空间中更小的变化。这促使模型捕捉代表数据中重要变化因素的特征，同时有效地忽略微小、不相关的波动或噪声。设想编码器将高维输入空间中的点映射到低维潜在空间；收缩映射确保输入空间中的邻域在映射到潜在空间时会收缩。 数学表述 为实现这种不敏感性，CAEs 在标准重建损失中添加一个惩罚项。此惩罚衡量编码器输出 h = f ( x ) h = f(x) h = f ( x ) 响应输入 x x x 的无穷小变化而变化的程度。这种敏感性由编码器函数 f f f 关于 x x x 的雅可比矩阵捕获。 雅可比矩阵 J ( x ) J(x) J ( x ) 是一个矩阵，包含编码器输出向量 (vector) h h h 相对于输入向量 x x x 的所有一阶偏导数： J i j ( x ) = ∂ h i ∂ x j J_{ij}(x) = \frac{\partial h_i}{\partial x_j} J ij ​ ( x ) = ∂ x j ​ ∂ h i ​ ​ 其中 h i h_i h i ​ 是潜在表示的第 i i i 个元素， x j x_j x j ​ 是输入的第 j j j 个元素。 收缩自编码器添加的惩罚与该雅可比矩阵的平方弗罗贝尼乌斯范数成比例。矩阵 A A A 的弗罗贝尼乌斯范数 ∣ ∣ A ∣ ∣ F ||A||F ∣∣ A ∣ ∣ F ​ 定义为 ∣ ∣ A ∣ ∣ F = ∑ i , j A i j 2 ||A||_F = \sqrt{\sum A_{ij}^2} ∣∣ A ∣ ∣ F ​ = ∑ i , j ​ A ij 2 ​ ​ 。因此，惩罚项为： Ω C A E ( x ) = ∣ ∣ J ( x ) ∣ ∣ F 2 = ∑ i , j ( ∂ h i ( x ) ∂ x j ) 2 \Omega_{CAE}(x) = ||J(x)||F^2 = \sum \left( \frac{\partial h_i(x)}{\partial x_j} \right)^2 Ω C A E ​ ( x ) = ∣∣ J ( x ) ∣ ∣ F 2 ​ = i , j ∑ ​ ( ∂ x j ​ ∂ h i ​ ( x ) ​ ) 2 该项对潜在特征相对于输入的所有偏导数的平方求和。最小化此项促使这些导数变小，使映射 f ( x ) f(x) f ( x ) 具有收缩性。 收缩自编码器的完整损失函数 (loss function)是重建损失（例如，均方误差或二元交叉熵）与此收缩惩罚之和，由超参数 (parameter) (hyperparameter) λ \lambda λ 加权： L C A E ( x , x ^ ) = L r e c ( x , x ^ ) + λ Ω C A E ( x ) L_{CAE}(x, \hat{x}) = L_{rec}(x, \hat{x}) + \lambda \Omega_{CAE}(x) L C A E ​ ( x , x ^ ) = L rec ​ ( x , x ^ ) + λ Ω C A E ​ ( x ) L C A E ( x , x ^ ) = L r e c ( x , x ^ ) + λ ∑ i , j ( ∂ h i ( x ) ∂ x j ) 2 L_{CAE}(x, \hat{x}) = L_{rec}(x, \hat{x}) + \lambda \sum_{i,j} \left( \frac{\partial h_i(x)}{\partial x_j} \right)^2 L C A E ​ ( x , x ^ ) = L rec ​ ( x , x ^ ) + λ i , j ∑ ​ ( ∂ x j ​ ∂ h i ​ ( x ) ​ ) 2 其中， x ^ = g ( f ( x ) ) \hat{x} = g(f(x)) x ^ = g ( f ( x )) 是重建输出， L r e c L_{rec} L rec ​ 是重建损失， λ > 0 \lambda > 0 λ > 0 控制收缩惩罚的强度。较大的 λ \lambda λ 会强制更强的收缩，但如果设置过高，可能会影响重建质量。调整 λ \lambda λ 有助于平衡学习不敏感表示与准确重建输入数据之间的权衡。 解释与流形学习的联系 最小化雅可比范数促使编码器 f ( x ) f(x) f ( x ) 主要在训练数据点附近具有收缩性。这与流形学习存在有趣的联系。如果数据位于高维输入空间中的低维流形上或附近，CAE 倾向于学习捕获沿流形变化的特征，同时收缩（对）与流形 正交 的方向（不敏感）。本质上，该惩罚促使编码器局部学习数据流形的切空间。 收缩映射的示意图。输入空间中微小的扰动 δ x \delta x δ x 应该导致潜在空间中更小的扰动 δ h \delta h δ h ，这是通过最小化编码器 f f f 的雅可比范数实现的。 实现考量 计算完整的雅可比矩阵及其弗罗贝尼乌斯范数会给训练过程带来显著的计算开销，特别是对于高维输入和潜在空间。幸运的是，现代深度学习 (deep learning)框架凭借自动微分能力可以高效地计算这种惩罚。虽然精确计算可能仍比简单的重建损失慢，但对于典型网络规模而言通常是可行的。框架通常提供优化的方法来计算平方梯度和或使用近似方法，避免显式构建完整的雅可比矩阵。 与去噪自编码器的比较 收缩自编码器和去噪自编码器都旨在学习对输入变化不太敏感的表示。然而，它们实现此目标的方式不同： DAEs: 隐式地 学习鲁棒性，通过训练模型从随机损坏的版本重建原始输入。模型必须学习足够稳定的特征，以忽略训练期间引入的特定类型噪声。 CAEs: 显式地 学习鲁棒性，通过添加惩罚项直接最小化所学特征相对于输入扰动 所有 方向的敏感性。 DAE 和 CAE 之间的选择可能取决于具体任务和数据中预期变化的性质。CAE 提供了一种更直接的分析方式来强制不敏感性，而 DAE 可能更直观，有时根据所选噪声模型更易于实现。 总之，收缩自编码器提供了一种数学上有依据的正则化 (regularization)方法，通过惩罚编码器映射的敏感性。这促使模型学习捕捉数据核心结构，同时对微小的局部扰动保持不变性的表示，有助于更好的特征学习。 这部分内容有帮助吗？ 有帮助 报告问题 标记为完成 参考文献 Contractive Auto-Encoders: Explicitly Promoting Small Derivatives of the Code Function , Salah Rifai, Pascal Vincent, Xavier Muller, Xavier Glorot, and Yoshua Bengio , 2011 JMLR Workshop and Conference Proceedings , Vol. 15 ( JMLR ) - 介绍收缩自编码器及其数学公式（包括雅可比惩罚）的基础论文。 Deep Learning , Ian Goodfellow, Yoshua Bengio, and Aaron Courville , 2016 ( MIT Press ) - 一本综合性教科书，在深度学习的广泛背景下涵盖了自编码器，包括收缩自编码器及其理论基础。 Representation Learning: A Review and New Perspectives , Yoshua Bengio, Aaron Courville, and Pascal Vincent , 2013 IEEE Transactions on Pattern Analysis and Machine Intelligence , Vol. 35 DOI: 10.48550/arXiv.1206.5538 - 一篇综述文章，讨论了各种表示学习技术，包括收缩自编码器，以及它们与流形学习等概念的关系。 © 2026 ApX Machine Learning AI伦理与透明度 •

33. Cooperative Deep Reinforcement Learning for Fair RIS Allocation

  • 链接：https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.25572v1
  • 来源：arxiv
  • 摘要：The deployment of reconfigurable intelligent surfaces (RISs) introduces new challenges for resource allocation in multi-cell wireless networks, particularly when user loads are uneven across base stations. In this work, we consider RISs as shared infrastructure that must be dynamically assigned among competing base stations, and we address this problem using a simultaneous ascending auction mechanism. To mitigate performance imbalances between cells, we propose a fairness-aware collaborative multi-agent reinforcement learning approach in which base stations adapt their bidding strategies based on both expected utility gains and relative service quality. A centrally computed performance-dependent fairness indicator is incorporated into the agents' observations, enabling implicit coordination without direct inter-base-station communication. Simulation results show that the proposed framework effectively redistributes RIS resources toward weaker-performing cells, substantially improving the rates of the worst-served users while preserving overall throughput. The results demonstrate that fairness-oriented RIS allocation can be achieved through cooperative learning, providing a flexible
  • 易漏细节梳理：

RISs的部署增加了多小区无线网络中资源分配的复杂性，这使得公平性指标成为关键因素。公平性指标是根据网络性能计算的，直接影响智能体的观察，进而使智能体能够进行隐式协调，而无需直接的基站间通信。基站根据预期的收益和相对的服务质量调整其出价策略，通过合作学习实现公平性导向的RIS分配。这种方法特别在最弱性能的小区中重新分配RIS资源，显著提高了最差服务用户的速率，同时整体吞吐量保持不变。因此，合作学习提供了一个灵活的工具，用于平衡未来无线网络中的效率和公平性，确保资源分配更加合理和高效。

  • 关键点（易漏细节）：
  • RISs的部署增加了多小区无线网络中资源分配的复杂性。
  • 公平性指标是根据网络性能计算的，影响智能体的观察。
  • 公平性指标使智能体能够进行隐式协调，而无需直接的基站间通信。
  • 基站根据预期的收益和相对的服务质量调整其出价策略。
  • 公平性导向的RIS分配可以通过合作学习实现。
  • 该方法在最弱性能的小区中重新分配RIS资源，显著提高了最差服务用户的速率。
  • 整体吞吐量在重新分配RIS资源后保持不变。
  • 合作学习提供了一个灵活的工具，用于平衡未来无线网络中的效率和公平性。

In this work, we consider RISs as shared infrastructure that must be dynamically assigned among competing base stations, and we address this problem using a simultaneous ascending auction mechanism. To mitigate performance imbalances between cells, we propose a fairness-aware collaborative multi-agent reinforcement learning approach in which base stations adapt their bidding strategies based on both expected utility gains and relative service quality. A centrally computed performance-dependent fairness indicator is incorporated into the agents' observations, enabling implicit coordination without direct inter-base-station communication. Simulation results show that the proposed framework effectively redistributes RIS resources toward weaker-performing cells, substantially improving the rates of the worst-served users while preserving overall throughput. The results demonstrate that fairness-oriented RIS allocation can be achieved through cooperative learning, providing a flexible tool for balancing efficiency and equity in future wireless networks. 34. A Mamba-based Perceptual Loss Function for Learning-based UGC Transcoding

  • 链接：https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.25566v1
  • 来源：arxiv
  • 摘要：In user-generated content (UGC) transcoding, source videos typically suffer various degradations due to prior compression, editing, or suboptimal capture conditions. Consequently, existing video compression paradigms that solely optimize for fidelity relative to the reference become suboptimal, as they force the codec to replicate the inherent artifacts of the non-pristine source. To address this, we propose a novel perceptually inspired loss function for learning-based UGC video transcoding that redefines the role of the reference video, shifting it from a ground-truth pixel anchor to an informative contextual guide. Specifically, we train a lightweight neural quality model based on a Selective Structured State-Space Model (Mamba) optimized using a weakly-supervised Siamese ranking strategy. The proposed model is then integrated into the rate-distortion optimization (RDO) process of two neural video codecs (DCVC and HiNeRV) as a loss function, aiming to generate reconstructed content with improved perceptual quality. Our experiments demonstrate that this framework achieves substantial coding gains over both autoencoder and implicit neural representation-based baselines, with 8.46%
  • 易漏细节梳理：

参考视频的角色从像素的真实锚点转变为有信息的上下文引导，这使得编码器生成的内容质量提升依赖于感知模型的训练。Mamba模型优化采用了弱监督的Siamese排名策略，进一步提升了编码效率。实验结果表明，该方法在编码效率上优于自动编码器和隐式神经表示基线，具体在BD-rate上分别节省了8.46%和12.89%。轻量级神经质量模型基于选择性结构化状态空间模型（Mamba），通过率失真优化过程中的损失函数，有助于提高感知质量。相比之下，现有视频压缩方法仅优化与参考的保真度，导致非纯净源的固有缺陷被复制，因此，新的方法能够更有效地处理非纯净源。

  • 关键点（易漏细节）：
  • 参考视频不再是像素的真实锚点，而是变成了有信息的上下文引导。
  • 编码器生成的内容质量提升依赖于感知模型的训练。
  • Mamba模型优化使用了弱监督的Siamese排名策略。
  • 率失真优化过程中的损失函数有助于提高感知质量。
  • 实验表明，该方法在编码效率上优于自动编码器和隐式神经表示基线。
  • 参考视频的角色被重新定义，从像素的真实锚点变为有信息的上下文引导。
  • 轻量级神经质量模型基于选择性结构化状态空间模型（Mamba）。
  • Siamese排名策略用于优化Mamba模型。
  • 该框架在BD-rate上分别节省了8.46%和12.89%。
  • 现有视频压缩方法仅优化与参考的保真度，导致非纯净源的固有缺陷被复制。

To address this, we propose a novel perceptually inspired loss function for learning-based UGC video transcoding that redefines the role of the reference video, shifting it from a ground-truth pixel anchor to an informative contextual guide. 35. Identifiable Deep Latent Variable Models for MNAR Data

  • 链接：https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.24771v1
  • 来源：arxiv
  • 摘要：Missing data is a ubiquitous challenge in data analysis, often leading to biased and inaccurate results. Traditional imputation methods usually assume that the missingness mechanism is missing-at-random (MAR), where the missingness is independent of the missing values themselves. This assumption is frequently violated in real-world scenarios, prompted by recent advances in imputation methods using deep learning to address this challenge. However, these methods neglect the crucial issue of nonparametric identifiability in missing-not-at-random (MNAR) data, which can lead to biased and unreliable results. This paper seeks to bridge this gap by proposing a novel framework based on deep latent variable models for {MNAR data}. Building on the assumption of conditional no self-censoring {given} latent variables, we establish the identifiability of the data distribution. This crucial theoretical result guarantees the feasibility of our approach. To effectively estimate unknown parameters, we develop an efficient algorithm utilizing importance-weighted autoencoders. We demonstrate, both theoretically and empirically, that our estimation process accurately recovers the ground-truth joint di
  • 易漏细节梳理：

在实际应用场景中，缺失机制往往违反了马尔可夫条件（MAR），这会导致非条件下的无偏估计变得困难。非条件下的无偏估计（MNAR）数据可能导致结果的偏差和不可靠性。在这种情况下，非参数可识别性变得至关重要，但往往被忽视。研究假设在条件下的无自我截断现象给定潜在变量，这一假设确保了理论结果的可识别性，从而保证了方法的可行性。为此，研究人员开发了重要加权自动编码器来估计参数，这一过程能够准确地恢复真实联合分布。特定的正则性条件进一步确保了准确的恢复。通过模拟研究和实际数据实验，该方法展示了其优势，与经典的和最先进的方法相比，其表现更为出色。

  • 关键点（易漏细节）：
  • missingness mechanism being MAR is often violated in real-world scenarios.
  • MNAR data can lead to biased and unreliable results.
  • nonparametric identifiability is crucial but often neglected in MNAR data.
  • conditional no self-censoring given latent variables is assumed.
  • theoretical result on identifiability guarantees the approach's feasibility.
  • importance-weighted autoencoders are developed for parameter estimation.
  • estimation process accurately recovers the ground-truth joint distribution.
  • specific regularity conditions ensure accurate recovery.
  • simulation studies and real-world data experiments showcase advantages.
  • classical and state-of-the-art approaches are compared unfavorably.

[2603.24771v1] Identifiable Deep Latent Variable Models for MNAR Data Statistics > Methodology arXiv:2603.24771v1 (stat) [Submitted on 25 Mar 2026] Title: Identifiable Deep Latent Variable Models for MNAR Data Authors: Huiming Xie , Fei Xue , Xiao Wang View a PDF of the paper titled Identifiable Deep Latent Variable Models for MNAR Data, by Huiming Xie and 2 other authors View PDF HTML (experimental) Abstract: Missing data is a ubiquitous challenge in data analysis, often leading to biased and inaccurate results. Traditional imputation methods usually assume that the missingness mechanism is missing-at-random (MAR), where the missingness is independent of the missing values themselves. This assumption is frequently violated in real-world scenarios, prompted by recent advances in imputation methods using deep learning to address this challenge. However, these methods neglect the crucial issue of nonparametric identifiability in missing-not-at-random (MNAR) data, which can lead to biased and unreliable results. This paper seeks to bridge this gap by proposing a novel framework based on deep latent variable models for {MNAR data}. Building on the assumption of conditional no self-censoring {given} latent variables, we establish the identifiability of the data distribution. This crucial theoretical result guarantees the feasibility of our approach. To effectively estimate unknown parameters, we develop an efficient algorithm utilizing importance-weighted autoencoders. We demonstrate, both theoretically and empirically, that our estimation process accurately recovers the ground-truth joint distribution under specific regularity conditions. Extensive simulation studies and real-world data experiments showcase the advantages of our proposed method compared to various classical and state-of-the-art approaches to missing data imputation. 36. EcoThink: A Green Adaptive Inference Framework for Sustainable and Accessible Agents

  • 链接：https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.25498v1
  • 来源：arxiv
  • 摘要：As the Web transitions from static retrieval to generative interaction, the escalating environmental footprint of Large Language Models (LLMs) presents a critical sustainability challenge. Current paradigms indiscriminately apply computation-intensive strategies like Chain-of-Thought (CoT) to billions of daily queries, causing LLM overthinking, a redundancy that amplifies carbon emissions and operational barriers. This inefficiency directly undermines UN Sustainable Development Goals 13 (Climate Action) and 10 (Reduced Inequalities) by hindering equitable AI access in resource-constrained regions. To address this, we introduce EcoThink, an energy-aware adaptive inference framework designed to reconcile high-performance AI intelligence with environmental responsibility. EcoThink employs a lightweight, distillation-based router to dynamically assess query complexity, skipping unnecessary reasoning for factoid retrieval while reserving deep computation for complex logic. Extensive evaluations across 9 diverse benchmarks demonstrate that EcoThink reduces inference energy by 40.4% on average (up to 81.9% for web knowledge retrieval) without statistically significant performance loss. By
  • 易漏细节梳理：

首先，LLMs的计算密集型策略会显著增加碳排放，这成为可持续发展的一大挑战。其次，EcoThink通过动态评估查询复杂性来减少不必要的推理，从而有效降低了能耗。EcoThink特别适用于事实检索，但在复杂逻辑处理时仍保留深度计算，确保了系统的灵活性和准确性。研究表明，EcoThink在9个基准测试中平均减少了40.4%的推理能耗，对于网络知识检索最多可减少81.9%的能耗。因此，EcoThink不仅有助于实现可持续发展目标13和10，还通过减少算法浪费，提供了一条可扩展的路径。此外，EcoThink在性能上没有统计意义上的损失，这进一步增强了其在实际应用中的优势。

  • 关键点（易漏细节）：
  • LLMs的计算密集型策略会增加碳排放。
  • EcoThink通过动态评估查询复杂性来减少不必要的推理。
  • EcoThink适用于事实检索，但保留深度计算用于复杂逻辑。
  • EcoThink在9个基准测试中平均减少40.4%的推理能耗。
  • EcoThink对于网络知识检索最多可减少81.9%的能耗。
  • EcoThink有助于实现可持续发展目标13和10。
  • EcoThink通过减少算法浪费，提供了一条可扩展的路径。
  • EcoThink在性能上没有统计意义上的损失。

37. Gap Safe Screening Rules for Fast Training of Robust Support Vector Machines under Feature Noise

  • 链接：https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.25221v1
  • 来源：arxiv
  • 摘要：Robust Support Vector Machines (R-SVMs) address feature noise by adopting a worst-case robust formulation that explicitly incorporates uncertainty sets into training. While this robustness improves reliability, it also leads to increased computational cost. In this work, we develop safe sample screening rules for R-SVMs that reduce the training complexity without affecting the optimal solution. To the best of our knowledge, this is the first study to apply safe screening techniques to worst-case robust models in supervised machine learning. Our approach safely identifies training samples whose uncertainty sets are guaranteed to lie entirely on either side of the margin hyperplane, thereby reducing the problem size and accelerating optimization. Owing to the nonstandard structure of R-SVMs, the proposed screening rules are derived from the Lagrangian duality rather than the Fenchel-Rockafellar duality commonly used in recent methods. Based on this analysis, we first establish an ideal screening rule, and then derive a practical rule by adapting GAP-based safe regions to the robust setting. Experiments demonstrate that the proposed method significantly reduces training time while pre
  • 易漏细节梳理：

safe screening规则能够通过减少训练复杂性来降低模型的训练难度，同时不会影响最优解，这使得安全筛选成为优化过程中的一个重要工具。R-SVMs（鲁棒支持向量机）的鲁棒形式明确地包含了不确定性集，这种非标准结构导致了不同的推导方法。实验结果表明，所提出的方法显著减少了训练时间，同时保持了分类准确性。首次研究将安全筛选技术应用于最坏情况下的鲁棒模型，这是监督机器学习领域的一个重要突破。此外，safe样本筛选能够识别那些不确定性集完全位于边缘超平面两侧的样本，从而加速优化过程。因此，通过Lagrangian对偶性而非Fenchel-Rockafellar对偶性推导出的安全筛选规则，不仅能够减少问题规模，还能提高训练效率，这是在鲁棒模型中应用安全筛选技术的首次尝试。

  • 关键点（易漏细节）：
  • safe screening rules can reduce training complexity without affecting the optimal solution.
  • the robust formulation of R-SVMs explicitly incorporates uncertainty sets.
  • the proposed screening rules are derived from Lagrangian duality, not Fenchel-Rockafellar duality.
  • safe sample screening identifies samples whose uncertainty sets lie entirely on either side of the margin hyperplane.
  • the nonstandard structure of R-SVMs leads to different derivation methods.
  • gap safe screening rules accelerate optimization by reducing the problem size.
  • experiments show the proposed method significantly reduces training time.
  • the method preserves classification accuracy while reducing training time.
  • this is the first study to apply safe screening techniques to worst-case robust models in supervised machine learning.

[2603.25221v1] Gap Safe Screening Rules for Fast Training of Robust Support Vector Machines under Feature Noise Computer Science > Machine Learning arXiv:2603.25221v1 (cs) [Submitted on 26 Mar 2026] Title: Gap Safe Screening Rules for Fast Training of Robust Support Vector Machines under Feature Noise Authors: Tan-Hau Nguyen , Thu-Le Tran , Kien Trung Nguyen View a PDF of the paper titled Gap Safe Screening Rules for Fast Training of Robust Support Vector Machines under Feature Noise, by Tan-Hau Nguyen and 2 other authors View PDF HTML (experimental) Abstract: Robust Support Vector Machines (R-SVMs) address feature noise by adopting a worst-case robust formulation that explicitly incorporates uncertainty sets into training. While this robustness improves reliability, it also leads to increased computational cost. In this work, we develop safe sample screening rules for R-SVMs that reduce the training complexity without affecting the optimal solution. 38. Unleashing Guidance Without Classifiers for Human-Object Interaction Animation

  • 链接：https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.25734v1
  • 来源：arxiv
  • 摘要：Generating realistic human-object interaction (HOI) animations remains challenging because it requires jointly modeling dynamic human actions and diverse object geometries. Prior diffusion-based approaches often rely on hand-crafted contact priors or human-imposed kinematic constraints to improve contact quality. We propose LIGHT, a data-driven alternative in which guidance emerges from the denoising pace itself, reducing dependence on manually designed priors. Building on diffusion forcing, we factor the representation into modality-specific components and assign individualized noise levels with asynchronous denoising schedules. In this paradigm, cleaner components guide noisier ones through cross-attention, yielding guidance without auxiliary classifiers. We find that this data-driven guidance is inherently contact-aware, and can be enhanced when training is augmented with a broad spectrum of synthetic object geometries, encouraging invariance of contact semantics to geometric diversity. Extensive experiments show that pace-induced guidance more effectively mirrors the benefits of contact priors than conventional classifier-free guidance, while achieving higher contact fidelity,
  • 易漏细节梳理：

指导并非依赖于人工设计的先验知识，而是通过数据驱动的方式实现。Cleaner组件通过交叉注意力引导noisier组件，从而实现更有效的接触先验模仿。异步去噪调度有助于增强接触先验的效果，而培训时增加合成对象几何多样性可以提高接触先验的不变性。此外，速度诱导的指导比传统无分类器指导更有效地模仿接触先验的好处，无分类器指导不仅能够实现更高的接触保真度，还能生成更真实的HOI动画，并增强对未见对象和任务的泛化能力。因此，数据驱动的指导方式不仅具有接触感知性，还能显著提升模型的性能和泛化能力。

  • 关键点（易漏细节）：
  • 指导并非依赖于人工设计的先验知识。
  • Cleaner组件通过交叉注意力引导noisier组件。
  • 数据驱动的指导本身具有接触感知性。
  • 异步去噪调度有助于增强接触先验的效果。
  • 培训时增加合成对象几何多样性可以提高接触先验的不变性。
  • 速度诱导的指导比传统无分类器指导更有效地模仿接触先验的好处。
  • 无分类器指导能实现更高的接触保真度。
  • 无分类器指导能生成更真实的HOI动画。
  • 无分类器指导能增强对未见对象和任务的泛化能力。

39. Vortex-driven superconducting diode effect in asymmetric multilayer heterostructures

  • 链接：https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.25147v1
  • 来源：arxiv
  • 摘要：The superconducting diode effect (SDE), characterized by nonreciprocal critical currents, has attracted growing attention due to its potential applications in quantum technologies and energy-efficient devices. In this work, we explore the microscopic mechanism of the SDE by simulating asymmetric multilayer heterostructures within time-dependent Ginzburg-Landau theory. We systematically vary the layer thickness, external magnetic field and stacking order in a trilayer structure composed of niobium, vanadium, and tantalum, which share a similar structure to that in the pioneering experimental work, to clarify the role of vortex dynamics. Our simulations reveal a pronounced SDE originating from the interplay of Lorentz forces and asymmetric vortex dynamics, which strongly depend on layer stacking order. Besides, by simply changing the stacking order of the constituent layers, the SDE can be entirely suppressed. These findings offer insights into the microscopic mechanisms of the SDE and provide a feasible approach for controlling and eliminating the SDE in practical superconducting devices.
  • 易漏细节梳理：

SDE的非互易临界电流特性依赖于层堆叠顺序，这表明通过调整层堆叠顺序可以有效控制SDE。具体而言，改变层堆叠顺序可以完全抑制SDE，这进一步说明了涡旋动力学在SDE中的关键作用。Lorentz力和非对称涡旋动力学的相互作用是导致SDE的原因之一。因此，通过简单改变层堆叠顺序，可以实现对SDE的有效控制和消除。

  • 关键点（易漏细节）：
  • SDE的非互易临界电流特性依赖于层堆叠顺序。
  • 改变层堆叠顺序可以完全抑制SDE。
  • Lorentz力和非对称涡旋动力学的相互作用导致了SDE。
  • 涡旋动力学在SDE中起关键作用。
  • SDE可以通过简单改变层堆叠顺序来控制和消除。

[2603.25147v1] Vortex-driven superconducting diode effect in asymmetric multilayer heterostructures Condensed Matter > Superconductivity arXiv:2603.25147v1 (cond-mat) [Submitted on 26 Mar 2026] Title: Vortex-driven superconducting diode effect in asymmetric multilayer heterostructures Authors: Jiong Li , Ji Jiang , Qing-Hu Chen View a PDF of the paper titled Vortex-driven superconducting diode effect in asymmetric multilayer heterostructures, by Jiong Li and 2 other authors View PDF HTML (experimental) Abstract: The superconducting diode effect (SDE), characterized by nonreciprocal critical currents, has attracted growing attention due to its potential applications in quantum technologies and energy-efficient devices. In this work, we explore the microscopic mechanism of the SDE by simulating asymmetric multilayer heterostructures within time-dependent Ginzburg-Landau theory. We systematically vary the layer thickness, external magnetic field and stacking order in a trilayer structure composed of niobium, vanadium, and tantalum, which share a similar structure to that in the pioneering experimental work, to clarify the role of vortex dynamics. Our simulations reveal a pronounced SDE originating from the interplay of Lorentz forces and asymmetric vortex dynamics, which strongly depend on layer stacking order. Besides, by simply changing the stacking order of the constituent layers, the SDE can be entirely suppressed. These findings offer insights into the microscopic mechanisms of the SDE and provide a feasible approach for controlling and eliminating the SDE in practical superconducting devices. 40. Anchored-Branched Steady-state WInd Flow Transformer (AB-SWIFT): a metamodel for 3D atmospheric flow in urban environments

  • 链接：https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.25635v1
  • 来源：arxiv
  • 摘要：Air flow modeling at a local scale is essential for applications such as pollutant dispersion modeling or wind farm modeling. To circumvent costly Computational Fluid Dynamics (CFD) computations, deep learning surrogate models have recently emerged as promising alternatives. However, in the context of urban air flow, deep learning models struggle to adapt to the high variations of the urban geometry and to large mesh sizes. To tackle these challenges, we introduce Anchored Branched Steady-state WInd Flow Transformer (AB-SWIFT), a transformer-based model with an internal branched structure uniquely designed for atmospheric flow modeling. We train our model on a specially designed database of atmospheric simulations around randomised urban geometries and with a mixture of unstable, neutral, and stable atmospheric stratifications. Our model reaches the best accuracy on all predicted fields compared to state-of-the-art transformers and graph-based models. Our code and data is available at https://github.com/cerea-daml/abswift.
  • 易漏细节梳理：

AB-SWIFT模型是一种专门设计用于大气流动建模的模型，它特别针对城市几何的高变异性进行了优化，能够适应大网格尺寸，从而解决了CFD计算成本高的问题。该模型基于变压器架构，能够在预测所有字段上达到最佳准确性，并且相比其他最先进的变压器和图基模型更为准确。AB-SWIFT模型需要大量特定设计的数据库进行训练，这些训练数据包括随机城市几何和不同大气层结，确保了模型的广泛适用性和高精度。此外，AB-SWIFT模型的代码和数据已公开，这使得研究人员能够进一步优化和扩展该模型的应用范围。因此，AB-SWIFT模型在大气流动建模领域展现出了显著的优势和潜力。

  • 关键点（易漏细节）：
  • AB-SWIFT模型需要大量特定设计的数据库进行训练。
  • AB-SWIFT模型在预测所有字段上都达到了最佳准确性。
  • AB-SWIFT模型特别设计用于大气流动建模。
  • AB-SWIFT模型能够适应城市几何的高变异性。
  • AB-SWIFT模型能够处理大网格尺寸。
  • AB-SWIFT模型是基于变压器的。
  • AB-SWIFT模型的代码和数据已公开。
  • AB-SWIFT模型的训练数据包括随机城市几何和不同大气层结。
  • AB-SWIFT模型相比其他最先进的变压器和图基模型更准确。
  • AB-SWIFT模型旨在解决CFD计算成本高的问题。

41. Layer-Specific Lipschitz Modulation for Fault-Tolerant Multimodal Representation Learning

  • 链接：https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.25103v1
  • 来源：arxiv
  • 摘要：Modern multimodal systems deployed in industrial and safety-critical environments must remain reliable under partial sensor failures, signal degradation, or cross-modal inconsistencies. This work introduces a mathematically grounded framework for fault-tolerant multimodal representation learning that unifies self-supervised anomaly detection and error correction within a single architecture. Building upon a theoretical analysis of perturbation propagation, we derive Lipschitz- and Jacobian-based criteria that determine whether a neural operator amplifies or attenuates localized faults. Guided by this theory, we propose a two-stage self-supervised training scheme: pre-training a multimodal convolutional autoencoder on clean data to preserve localized anomaly signals in the latent space, and expanding it with a learnable compute block composed of dense layers for correction and contrastive objectives for anomaly identification. Furthermore, we introduce layer-specific Lipschitz modulation and gradient clipping as principled mechanisms to control sensitivity across detection and correction modules. Experimental results on multimodal fault datasets demonstrate that the proposed approac
  • 易漏细节梳理：

Lipschitz-和Jacobian-based criteria能够判断神经算子是放大还是减弱局部故障，从而帮助识别潜在的异常信号。为了进一步控制检测和修正模块间的灵敏度，引入了Layer-specific Lipschitz modulation机制，通过调整不同层的灵敏度来优化异常检测的准确性。此外，Gradient clipping作为一种控制灵敏度的机制，有助于防止过拟合，进一步提升模型的鲁棒性。在预训练阶段，保留了局部异常信号在潜在空间中的特征，使得模型能够更好地学习和识别异常。学习可调节计算块包含密集层进行修正和异常识别，通过密集层的调整来优化异常检测和修复的效果。实验结果表明，该方法不仅能够提高异常检测的准确性和传感器损坏下的重建效果，还填补了分析鲁棒性保证和实际故障容忍多模态学习之间的空白。

  • 关键点（易漏细节）：
  • Lipschitz-和Jacobian-based criteria能判断神经算子是放大还是减弱局部故障。
  • Layer-specific Lipschitz modulation能控制检测和修正模块间的灵敏度。
  • Gradient clipping是控制灵敏度的机制之一。
  • 预训练阶段保留了局部异常信号在潜在空间中。
  • 学习可调节计算块包含密集层进行修正和异常识别。
  • 实验结果表明该方法能提高异常检测准确性和传感器损坏下的重建。
  • 该框架填补了分析鲁棒性保证和实际故障容忍多模态学习之间的空白。

[2603.25103v1] Layer-Specific Lipschitz Modulation for Fault-Tolerant Multimodal Representation Learning Computer Science > Machine Learning arXiv:2603.25103v1 (cs) [Submitted on 26 Mar 2026] Title: Layer-Specific Lipschitz Modulation for Fault-Tolerant Multimodal Representation Learning Authors: Diyar Altinses , Andreas Schwung View a PDF of the paper titled Layer-Specific Lipschitz Modulation for Fault-Tolerant Multimodal Representation Learning, by Diyar Altinses and Andreas Schwung View PDF HTML (experimental) Abstract: Modern multimodal systems deployed in industrial and safety-critical environments must remain reliable under partial sensor failures, signal degradation, or cross-modal inconsistencies. This work introduces a mathematically grounded framework for fault-tolerant multimodal representation learning that unifies self-supervised anomaly detection and error correction within a single architecture. Building upon a theoretical analysis of perturbation propagation, we derive Lipschitz- and Jacobian-based criteria that determine whether a neural operator amplifies or attenuates localized faults. Guided by this theory, we propose a two-stage self-supervised training scheme: pre-training a multimodal convolutional autoencoder on clean data to preserve localized anomaly signals in the latent space, and expanding it with a learnable compute block composed of dense layers for correction and contrastive objectives for anomaly identification. Furthermore, we introduce layer-specific Lipschitz modulation and gradient clipping as principled mechanisms to control sensitivity across detection and correction modules. Experimental results on multimodal fault datasets demonstrate that the proposed approach improves both anomaly detection accuracy and reconstruction under sensor corruption. Overall, this framework bridges the gap between analytical robustness guarantees and practical fault-tolerant multimodal learning. 42. How Pruning Reshapes Features: Sparse Autoencoder Analysis of Weight-Pruned Language Models

  • 链接：https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.25325v1
  • 来源：arxiv
  • 摘要：Weight pruning is a standard technique for compressing large language models, yet its effect on learned internal representations remains poorly understood. We present the first systematic study of how unstructured pruning reshapes the feature geometry of language models, using Sparse Autoencoders (SAEs) as interpretability probes. Across three model families (Gemma 3 1B, Gemma 2 2B, Llama 3.2 1B), two pruning methods (magnitude and Wanda), and six sparsity levels (0--60%), we investigate five research questions spanning seed stability, feature survival, SAE transferability, feature fragility, and causal relevance. Our most striking finding is that rare SAE features--those with low firing rates--survive pruning far better than frequent ones, with within-condition Spearman correlations of rho = -1.0 in 11 of 17 experimental conditions. This counter-intuitive result suggests that pruning acts as implicit feature selection, preferentially destroying high-frequency generic features while preserving specialized rare ones. We further show that Wanda pruning preserves feature structure up to 3.7x better than magnitude pruning, that pre-trained SAEs remain viable on Wanda-pruned models up t
  • 易漏细节梳理：

pruning偏好保留高频的通用特征而破坏低频的特殊特征，这种倾向使得稀有SAE特征（低激活率）在剪枝后比常见特征更可能幸存。尽管如此，剪枝后的几何特征生存并不预测因果重要性，这在解释压缩下的可解释性中有重要影响。值得注意的是，预训练SAE在Wanda剪枝后模型中仍保持有效性，直到50%稀疏度，而稀有特征的生存率与常见特征有显著差异。此外，尽管pruning方法Wanda比magnitude更能保持特征结构，但剪枝对语言模型内部表示的影响尚未完全理解，这表明剪枝实际上作为隐含特征选择，破坏高频通用特征而保留特殊稀有特征。因此，稀有特征的生存率与常见特征的显著差异，以及剪枝对几何特征生存和因果重要性的无影响，共同揭示了剪枝在模型压缩中的复杂作用。

  • 关键点（易漏细节）：
  • pruning偏好保留高频的通用特征而破坏低频的特殊特征。
  • pruning方法Wanda比magnitude更能保持特征结构。
  • 稀有SAE特征（低激活率）在剪枝后比常见特征更可能幸存。
  • 剪枝后的几何特征生存并不预测因果重要性。
  • 预训练SAE在Wanda剪枝后模型中仍保持有效性，直到50%稀疏度。
  • 剪枝对语言模型内部表示的影响尚未完全理解。
  • 稀有特征的生存率与常见特征有显著差异。
  • 剪枝作为隐含特征选择，破坏高频通用特征而保留特殊稀有特征。
  • 几何特征生存并不预测因果重要性，这在解释压缩下的可解释性中有重要影响。

[2603.25325v1] How Pruning Reshapes Features: Sparse Autoencoder Analysis of Weight-Pruned Language Models Computer Science > Machine Learning arXiv:2603.25325v1 (cs) [Submitted on 26 Mar 2026] Title: How Pruning Reshapes Features: Sparse Autoencoder Analysis of Weight-Pruned Language Models Authors: Hector Borobia , Elies Seguí-Mas , Guillermina Tormo-Carbó View a PDF of the paper titled How Pruning Reshapes Features: Sparse Autoencoder Analysis of Weight-Pruned Language Models, by Hector Borobia and 2 other authors View PDF HTML (experimental) Abstract: Weight pruning is a standard technique for compressing large language models, yet its effect on learned internal representations remains poorly understood. 43. Spatiotemporal System Forecasting with Irregular Time Steps via Masked Autoencoder

  • 链接：https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.25597v1
  • 来源：arxiv
  • 摘要：Predicting high-dimensional dynamical systems with irregular time steps presents significant challenges for current data-driven algorithms. These irregularities arise from missing data, sparse observations, or adaptive computational techniques, reducing prediction accuracy. To address these limitations, we propose a novel method: a Physics-Spatiotemporal Masked Autoencoder. This method integrates convolutional autoencoders for spatial feature extraction with masked autoencoders optimised for irregular time series, leveraging attention mechanisms to reconstruct the entire physical sequence in a single prediction pass. The model avoids the need for data imputation while preserving physical integrity of the system. Here, 'physics' refers to high-dimensional fields generated by underlying dynamical systems, rather than the enforcement of explicit physical constraints or PDE residuals. We evaluate this approach on multiple simulated datasets and real-world ocean temperature data. The results demonstrate that our method achieves significant improvements in prediction accuracy, robustness to nonlinearities, and computational efficiency over traditional convolutional and recurrent network
  • 易漏细节梳理：

不规则的时间步长会导致预测精度降低，而缺失数据和稀疏观测则进一步增加了预测的挑战。这些不规则性源于适应性计算技术的应用，而数据驱动的算法在处理高维动态系统时往往表现不佳。在此背景下，物理概念指的是高维场，而非显式的约束条件。注意力机制有助于重建整个物理序列，从而避免了数据填充的需要，并保持了系统的物理完整性。这种方法在预测精度上取得了显著的改进，并展示了对非线性的鲁棒性和计算效率。它在气候建模等多个领域具有潜在应用，能够捕捉复杂的时空模式，而无需特定领域的知识。该方法在模拟和实际海洋温度数据上进行了评估，展示了其在预测准确性、非线性鲁棒性和计算效率方面的优势。

  • 关键点（易漏细节）：
  • irregular time steps can lead to reduced prediction accuracy.
  • missing data and sparse observations contribute to prediction challenges.
  • adaptive computational techniques can cause irregularities.
  • data-driven algorithms struggle with high-dimensional dynamical systems.
  • physics in this context refers to high-dimensional fields, not explicit constraints.
  • attention mechanisms help reconstruct the entire physical sequence.
  • the method avoids the need for data imputation.
  • it preserves the physical integrity of the system.
  • the model demonstrates significant improvements in prediction accuracy.
  • it shows robustness to nonlinearities and computational efficiency.
  • it has potential applications in various fields like climate modeling.
  • it can capture complex spatiotemporal patterns without domain-specific knowledge.
  • the approach is evaluated on simulated and real-world ocean temperature data.

44. THEMIS: Towards Holistic Evaluation of MLLMs for Scientific Paper Fraud Forensics

  • 链接：https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.25089v1
  • 来源：arxiv
  • 摘要：We present THEMIS, a novel multi-task benchmark designed to comprehensively evaluate multimodal large language models (MLLMs) on visual fraud reasoning within real-world academic scenarios. Compared to existing benchmarks, THEMIS introduces three major advances. (1) Real-World Scenarios and Complexity: Our benchmark comprises over 4,000 questions spanning seven scenarios, derived from authentic retracted-paper cases and carefully curated multimodal synthetic data. With 60.47% complex-texture images, THEMIS bridges the critical gap between existing benchmarks and the complexity of real-world academic fraud. (2) Fraud-Type Diversity and Granularity: THEMIS systematically covers five challenging fraud types and introduces 16 fine-grained manipulation operations. On average, each sample undergoes multiple stacked manipulation operations, with the diversity and difficulty of these manipulations demanding a high level of visual fraud reasoning from the models. (3) Multi-Dimensional Capability Evaluation: We establish a mapping from fraud types to five core visual fraud reasoning capabilities, thereby enabling an evaluation that reveals the distinct strengths and specific weaknesses of di
  • 易漏细节梳理：

THEMIS是一个广泛且严格的测试框架，包含4000多个问题，覆盖七个真实场景，旨在评估模型在五种挑战性的欺诈类型上的表现。每个样本平均经历了多次叠加的篡改操作，这些操作包括16种精细的篡改方法，确保了测试的全面性和真实性。THEMIS评估了五种核心视觉欺诈推理能力，其中GPT-5在THEMIS上的整体性能仅为56.15%，这表明现有的模型在处理复杂的视觉欺诈时仍存在显著的不足。此外，THEMIS的数据来源于真实的撤稿论文案例，这使得测试更加贴近实际应用场景。因此，THEMIS不仅展示了对MLLMs的严格测试，还有助于识别不同模型的强项和弱点，从而推动模型性能的提升。

  • 关键点（易漏细节）：
  • THEMIS包含4000多个问题，覆盖七个真实场景。
  • 每个样本平均经历了多次叠加的篡改操作。
  • THEMIS评估了五种核心视觉欺诈推理能力。
  • GPT-5在THEMIS上的整体性能仅为56.15%。
  • THEMIS展示了对MLLMs的严格测试。
  • THEMIS的数据来自真实的撤稿论文案例。
  • THEMIS覆盖了五种挑战性的欺诈类型。
  • THEMIS引入了16种精细的篡改操作。
  • THEMIS有助于识别不同模型的强项和弱点。

Compared to existing benchmarks, THEMIS introduces three major advances. (1) Real-World Scenarios and Complexity: Our benchmark comprises over 4,000 questions spanning seven scenarios, derived from authentic retracted-paper cases and carefully curated multimodal synthetic data. With 60.47% complex-texture images, THEMIS bridges the critical gap between existing benchmarks and the complexity of real-world academic fraud. We expect THEMIS to advance the development of MLLMs for complex, real-world fraud reasoning tasks. 45. An Experimental Comparison of the Most Popular Approaches to Fake News Detection

  • 链接：https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.25501v1
  • 来源：arxiv
  • 摘要：In recent years, fake news detection has received increasing attention in public debate and scientific research. Despite advances in detection techniques, the production and spread of false information have become more sophisticated, driven by Large Language Models (LLMs) and the amplification power of social media. We present a critical assessment of 12 representative fake news detection approaches, spanning traditional machine learning, deep learning, transformers, and specialized cross-domain architectures. We evaluate these methods on 10 publicly available datasets differing in genre, source, topic, and labeling rationale. We address text-only English fake news detection as a binary classification task by harmonizing labels into "Real" and "Fake" to ensure a consistent evaluation protocol. We acknowledge that label semantics vary across datasets and that harmonization inevitably removes such semantic nuances. Each dataset is treated as a distinct domain. We conduct in-domain, multi-domain and cross-domain experiments to simulate real-world scenarios involving domain shift and out-of-distribution data. Fine-tuned models perform well in-domain but struggle to generalize. Cross-do
  • 易漏细节梳理：

label harmonization可能丢失原始标签的语义信息，这使得每个数据集被视为一个独立领域。fine-tuned模型在域内表现良好，但难以泛化到新领域。为减少泛化差距，cross-domain架构被提出，但其需要大量数据支持。此外，LLMs通过零样本和少量样本学习提供了另一种替代方案，使得模型在不同领域中也能表现出色。然而，这些结果应被视为在英语文本协议下的鲁棒性评估，因为数据集固有的混淆因素可能影响结果解释。预训练过程可能使模型暴露于特定数据集的偏差，进一步影响其泛化能力。因此，解决这些挑战需要综合考虑模型的泛化能力和数据集的多样性。

  • 关键点（易漏细节）：
  • label harmonization可能丢失原始标签的语义信息
  • 每个数据集被视为一个独立领域
  • fine-tuned模型在域内表现良好但难以泛化
  • cross-domain架构能减少泛化差距但需要大量数据
  • LLMs通过零样本和少量样本学习提供替代方案

46. Towards Controllable Low-Light Image Enhancement: A Continuous Multi-illumination Dataset and Efficient State Space Framework

  • 链接：https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.25296v1
  • 来源：arxiv
  • 摘要：Low-light image enhancement (LLIE) has traditionally been formulated as a deterministic mapping. However, this paradigm often struggles to account for the ill-posed nature of the task, where unknown ambient conditions and sensor parameters create a multimodal solution space. Consequently, state-of-the-art methods frequently encounter luminance discrepancies between predictions and labels, often necessitating "gt-mean" post-processing to align output luminance for evaluation. To address this fundamental limitation, we propose a transition toward Controllable Low-light Enhancement (CLE), explicitly reformulating the task as a well-posed conditional problem. To this end, we introduce CLE-RWKV, a holistic framework supported by Light100, a new benchmark featuring continuous real-world illumination transitions. To resolve the conflict between luminance control and chromatic fidelity, a noise-decoupled supervision strategy in the HVI color space is employed, effectively separating illumination modulation from texture restoration. Architecturally, to adapt efficient State Space Models (SSMs) for dense prediction, we leverage a Space-to-Depth (S2D) strategy. By folding spatial neighborhood
  • 易漏细节梳理：

确定性映射范式在处理低光照图像增强任务的病态性质时常常失效，因为未知的环境条件和传感器参数导致了多模态的解空间。因此，预测与标签之间的亮度差异在最先进的方法中很常见，而“gt-mean”后处理通常被要求来对齐输出亮度以进行评估。为了解决这一问题，可控低光照增强（CLE）明确地将任务重新表述为一个条件下的良好定义问题，即通过Light100这一新的基准，它支持了一个整体框架CLE-RWKV，该基准特征包括连续的现实世界照明过渡。此外，HVI颜色空间中的噪声解耦监督有效地分离了光照调制和纹理恢复。空间到深度（S2D）策略允许模型恢复局部归纳偏置并弥合“扫描间隙”，尽管这会导致扁平化视觉序列的潜在问题，但不会牺牲线性复杂度。实验结果表明，该方法在七个基准上表现出竞争力和稳健的可控性，显著减少了对“gt-mean”后处理的依赖。Light100为连续的现实世界照明过渡提供了一个新的基准。

  • 关键点（易漏细节）：
  • deterministic mapping paradigm often fails to handle the ill-posed nature of low-light image enhancement tasks.
  • unknown ambient conditions and sensor parameters create a multimodal solution space for low-light image enhancement.
  • luminance discrepancies between predictions and labels are common in state-of-the-art methods.
  • "gt-mean" post-processing is often required to align output luminance for evaluation.
  • controllable low-light enhancement (CLE) explicitly reformulates the task as a well-posed conditional problem.
  • CLE-RWKV is a holistic framework supported by Light100, a new benchmark featuring continuous real-world illumination transitions.
  • noise-decoupled supervision in the HVI color space effectively separates illumination modulation from texture restoration.
  • space-to-depth (S2D) strategy allows the model to recover local inductive biases and bridge the "scanning gap".
  • flattened visual sequences can be inherently problematic without sacrificing linear complexity.
  • experiments across seven benchmarks demonstrate competitive performance and robust controllability.
  • reliance on "gt-mean" post-processing is significantly reduced with the proposed approach.
  • light100 provides a new benchmark for continuous real-world illumination transitions.

[2603.25296v1] Towards Controllable Low-Light Image Enhancement: A Continuous Multi-illumination Dataset and Efficient State Space Framework Computer Science > Computer Vision and Pattern Recognition arXiv:2603.25296v1 (cs) [Submitted on 26 Mar 2026] Title: Towards Controllable Low-Light Image Enhancement: A Continuous Multi-illumination Dataset and Efficient State Space Framework Authors: Hongru Han , Tingrui Guo , Liming Zhang , Yan Su , Qiwen Xu , Zhuohua Ye View a PDF of the paper titled Towards Controllable Low-Light Image Enhancement: A Continuous Multi-illumination Dataset and Efficient State Space Framework, by Hongru Han and 5 other authors View PDF HTML (experimental) Abstract: Low-light image enhancement (LLIE) has traditionally been formulated as a deterministic mapping. However, this paradigm often struggles to account for the ill-posed nature of the task, where unknown ambient conditions and sensor parameters create a multimodal solution space. Consequently, state-of-the-art methods frequently encounter luminance discrepancies between predictions and labels, often necessitating "gt-mean" post-processing to align output luminance for evaluation. To address this fundamental limitation, we propose a transition toward Controllable Low-light Enhancement (CLE), explicitly reformulating the task as a well-posed conditional problem. To this end, we introduce CLE-RWKV, a holistic framework supported by Light100, a new benchmark featuring continuous real-world illumination transitions. To resolve the conflict between luminance control and chromatic fidelity, a noise-decoupled supervision strategy in the HVI color space is employed, effectively separating illumination modulation from texture restoration. Architecturally, to adapt efficient State Space Models (SSMs) for dense prediction, we leverage a Space-to-Depth (S2D) strategy. By folding spatial neighborhoods into channel dimensions, this design allows the model to recover local inductive biases and effectively bridge the "scanning gap" inherent in flattened visual sequences without sacrificing linear complexity. Experiments across seven benchmarks demonstrate that our approach achieves competitive performance and robust controllability, providing a real-world multi-illumination alternative that significantly reduces the reliance on gt-mean post-processing. 47. From Logic Monopoly to Social Contract: Separation of Power and the Institutional Foundations for Autonomous Agent Economies

  • 链接：https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.25100v1
  • 来源：arxiv
  • 摘要：Existing multi-agent frameworks allow each agent to simultaneously plan, execute, and evaluate its own actions -- a structural deficiency we term the "Logic Monopoly." Empirical evidence quantifies the resulting "Reliability Gap": 84.30% average attack success rates across ten deployment scenarios, 31.4% emergent deceptive behavior without explicit reward signals, and cascading failure modes rooted in six structural bottlenecks. The remedy is not better alignment of individual models but a social contract for agents: institutional infrastructure that enforces a constitutional Separation of Power. This paper introduces the Agent Enterprise for Enterprise (AE4E) paradigm -- agents as autonomous, legally identifiable business entities within a functionalist social system -- with a contract-centric SoP model trifurcating authority into Legislation, Execution, and Adjudication branches. The paradigm is operationalized through the NetX Enterprise Framework (NEF): governance hubs, TEE-backed compute enclaves, privacy-preserving data bridges, and an Agent-Native blockchain substrate. The Agent Enterprise Economy scales across four deployment tiers from private enclaves to a global Web of
  • 易漏细节梳理：

结构缺陷导致的 Logic Monopoly 是每个代理同时规划、执行和评估自身行为的结构缺陷，这使得高攻击成功率和隐秘欺骗行为成为可能。根源在于六个结构性瓶颈，这些瓶颈使得代理难以被有效监管和评估。因此，更好的模型对齐无法解决这一问题，需要通过社会合同来解决。社会合同通过分权制衡的方式，将权力分为立法、执行和司法三个分支，确保代理行为的可靠性。AE4E 帕拉范式将代理视为具有法律身份的业务实体，而 SoP 模型则进一步将权力分为立法、执行和司法三个分支，提供了一种治理机制。NetX 企业框架则提供了治理枢纽、TEE支持的计算 enclave、隐私保护数据桥梁和代理本位区块链，从私人 enclave 到全球 Web 服务，在四个部署层级上扩展。此外，Agentic 社会层基于帕森斯 AGIL 框架提供机构基础设施，AE4E 帕拉范式通过六十多个命名的机构 AE4E 提供基础设施，进一步增强了治理能力。因此，通过分权制衡的社会合同机制和 NetX 企业框架，可以有效解决结构缺陷带来的问题。

  • 关键点（易漏细节）：
  • Logic Monopoly 指每个代理同时规划、执行和评估自身行为的结构缺陷。
  • Reliability Gap 表现为高攻击成功率和隐秘欺骗行为，根源在于六个结构性瓶颈。
  • 更好的模型对齐无法解决 Reliability Gap，需要通过社会合同来解决。
  • 社会合同通过分权制衡来确保代理行为的可靠性。
  • AE4E 帕拉范式将代理视为具有法律身份的业务实体。
  • SoP 模型将权力分为立法、执行和司法三个分支。
  • NetX 企业框架提供治理枢纽、TEE支持的计算 enclave、隐私保护数据桥梁和代理本位区块链。
  • Agentic 社会层基于帕森斯 AGIL 框架提供机构基础设施。
  • AE4E 帕拉范式通过六十多个命名的机构 AE4E 提供基础设施。
  • NetX 企业框架在四个部署层级上扩展，从私人 enclave 到全球 Web 服务。
  • 结构缺陷导致高攻击成功率和隐秘欺骗行为，源于六个结构性瓶颈。

48. SEVerA: Verified Synthesis of Self-Evolving Agents

  • 链接：https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.25111v1
  • 来源：arxiv
  • 摘要：Recent advances have shown the effectiveness of self-evolving LLM agents on tasks such as program repair and scientific discovery. In this paradigm, a planner LLM synthesizes an agent program that invokes parametric models, including LLMs, which are then tuned per task to improve performance. However, existing self-evolving agent frameworks provide no formal guarantees of safety or correctness. Because such programs are often executed autonomously on unseen inputs, this lack of guarantees raises reliability and security concerns. We formulate agentic code generation as a constrained learning problem, combining hard formal specifications with soft objectives capturing task utility. We introduce Formally Guarded Generative Models (FGGM), which allow the planner LLM to specify a formal output contract for each generative model call using first-order logic. Each FGGM call wraps the underlying model in a rejection sampler with a verified fallback, ensuring every returned output satisfies the contract for any input and parameter setting. Building on FGGM, we present SEVerA (Self-Evolving Verified Agents), a three-stage framework: Search synthesizes candidate parametric programs containin
  • 易漏细节梳理：

SEVerA框架通过整合形式保证，有效解决了可靠性与安全性问题。首先，SEVerA框架中的正式输出合同确保每个返回输出都满足指定条件，从而保证了输出的质量。其次，拒绝采样器结合验证后备机制，进一步增强系统的可靠性，确保任何输入和参数设置下的正确性。搜索阶段合成包含FGGM调用的候选程序，增加了灵活性。验证阶段则证明了候选程序在硬约束下的正确性，将问题简化为无约束学习。学习阶段通过优化来改善软目标，同时保持正确性。SEVerA框架中的正式行为约束引导合成向更高质量的代理发展，而不仅仅是确保正确性。此外，SEVerA框架通过三阶段（搜索、验证、学习）系统性地解决了代理合成的不同方面，不仅改进了无约束和SOTA基线，还证明了其有效性。FGGM调用对于确保生成模型满足形式规范至关重要。因此，SEVerA框架通过这三个阶段的系统性方法，全面提升了代理合成的质量和可靠性。

  • 关键点（易漏细节）：
  • formal output contracts ensure every returned output satisfies the specified conditions.
  • rejection samplers with verified fallbacks enhance reliability by ensuring correctness for any input and parameter setting.
  • search stage synthesizes candidate programs containing FGGM calls, introducing flexibility.
  • verification stage proves correctness with respect to hard constraints, reducing the problem to unconstrained learning.
  • learning stage applies optimization to improve soft objectives while preserving correctness.
  • SEVerA framework addresses reliability and security concerns by incorporating formal guarantees.
  • formal behavioral constraints steer synthesis towards higher-quality agents, not just ensuring correctness.
  • unconstrained and SOTA baselines are improved by SEVerA, demonstrating its effectiveness.
  • FGGM calls are crucial for ensuring that generated models meet formal specifications.
  • three-stage framework (Search, Verification, Learning) systematically addresses different aspects of agent synthesis.

[2603.25111v1] SEVerA: Verified Synthesis of Self-Evolving Agents Computer Science > Machine Learning arXiv:2603.25111v1 (cs) [Submitted on 26 Mar 2026] Title: SEVerA: Verified Synthesis of Self-Evolving Agents Authors: Debangshu Banerjee , Changming Xu , Gagandeep Singh View a PDF of the paper titled SEVerA: Verified Synthesis of Self-Evolving Agents, by Debangshu Banerjee and 2 other authors View PDF HTML (experimental) Abstract: Recent advances have shown the effectiveness of self-evolving LLM agents on tasks such as program repair and scientific discovery. In this paradigm, a planner LLM synthesizes an agent program that invokes parametric models, including LLMs, which are then tuned per task to improve performance. However, existing self-evolving agent frameworks provide no formal guarantees of safety or correctness. Because such programs are often executed autonomously on unseen inputs, this lack of guarantees raises reliability and security concerns. We formulate agentic code generation as a constrained learning problem, combining hard formal specifications with soft objectives capturing task utility. We introduce Formally Guarded Generative Models (FGGM), which allow the planner LLM to specify a formal output contract for each generative model call using first-order logic. Each FGGM call wraps the underlying model in a rejection sampler with a verified fallback, ensuring every returned output satisfies the contract for any input and parameter setting. Building on FGGM, we present SEVerA (Self-Evolving Verified Agents), a three-stage framework: Search synthesizes candidate parametric programs containing FGGM calls; Verification proves correctness with respect to hard constraints for all parameter values, reducing the problem to unconstrained learning; and Learning applies scalable gradient-based optimization, including GRPO-style fine-tuning, to improve the soft objective while preserving correctness. We evaluate SEVerA on Dafny program verification, symbolic math synthesis, and policy-compliant agentic tool use ($\tau^2$-bench). Across tasks, SEVerA achieves zero constraint violations while improving performance over unconstrained and SOTA baselines, showing that formal behavioral constraints not only guarantee correctness but also steer synthesis toward higher-quality agents. 49. General-Purpose Machine-Learned Potential for CrCoNi Alloys Enabling Large-Scale Atomistic Simulations with First-Principles Accuracy

  • 链接：https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.25616v1
  • 来源：arxiv
  • 摘要：CrCoNi medium-entropy alloys exhibit exceptional mechanical properties arising from pronounced chemical complexity, including short-range order (SRO), and low stacking fault energy, posing challenges for large-scale atomistic simulations. While most models focus on equimolar compositions, deviations from equimolarity provide an effective route to tuning properties, requiring transferable interatomic potentials that capture composition-dependent behavior. Here we develop a general-purpose machine-learned interatomic potential for the CrCoNi system within the neuroevolution potential (NEP) framework, achieving near first-principles accuracy with high computational efficiency. Trained on a comprehensive dataset spanning pure elements, binary and ternary alloys across a wide compositional range, diverse crystal structures and thermodynamic conditions, and based on spin-polarized \textit{ab initio} data, the model accurately reproduces equations of state, phonons, elastic constants, dislocation dissociation, surface and defect energies, melting temperatures and strain-induced phase transformations. It further captures SRO and its effect on stacking fault energies across both equimolar a
  • 易漏细节梳理：

机器学习势能模型因其强大的能力而成为非等摩尔合金研究的重要工具。首先，它能够准确模拟纯元素、二元和三元合金，同时捕捉化学组成依赖的行为。其次，通过在不同晶体结构和热力学条件下进行训练，该模型能够准确再现方程状态、声子、弹性常数等关键物理性质。此外，机器学习势能模型还能够捕捉短程有序及其对堆叠能的影响，这在非等摩尔合金设计中尤为重要。因此，与现有模型相比，机器学习势能模型在计算效率上具有显著优势，并能够准确模拟等摩尔和非等摩尔合金。最后，该模型为非等摩尔CrCoNi合金设计提供了坚实的基础，使其成为合金设计和优化的重要框架。

  • 关键点（易漏细节）：
  • 机器学习势能模型可以处理非等摩尔合金。
  • 机器学习势能模型能够准确模拟纯元素、二元和三元合金。
  • 机器学习势能模型能够捕捉化学组成依赖的行为。
  • 机器学习势能模型在不同晶体结构和热力学条件下训练。
  • 机器学习势能模型能够准确再现方程状态、声子、弹性常数。
  • 机器学习势能模型能够捕捉短程有序及其对堆叠能的影响。
  • 机器学习势能模型在计算效率上优于现有模型。
  • 机器学习势能模型能够准确模拟等摩尔和非等摩尔合金。
  • 机器学习势能模型能够提供非等摩尔CrCoNi合金设计的框架。

[2603.25616v1] General-Purpose Machine-Learned Potential for CrCoNi Alloys Enabling Large-Scale Atomistic Simulations with First-Principles Accuracy Condensed Matter > Materials Science arXiv:2603.25616v1 (cond-mat) [Submitted on 26 Mar 2026] Title: General-Purpose Machine-Learned Potential for CrCoNi Alloys Enabling Large-Scale Atomistic Simulations with First-Principles Accuracy Authors: Yong-Chao Wu , Tero Mäkinen , Mikko Alava , Amin Esfandiarpour View a PDF of the paper titled General-Purpose Machine-Learned Potential for CrCoNi Alloys Enabling Large-Scale Atomistic Simulations with First-Principles Accuracy, by Yong-Chao Wu and Tero M\"akinen and Mikko Alava and Amin Esfandiarpour View PDF HTML (experimental) Abstract: CrCoNi medium-entropy alloys exhibit exceptional mechanical properties arising from pronounced chemical complexity, including short-range order (SRO), and low stacking fault energy, posing challenges for large-scale atomistic simulations. While most models focus on equimolar compositions, deviations from equimolarity provide an effective route to tuning properties, requiring transferable interatomic potentials that capture composition-dependent behavior. Here we develop a general-purpose machine-learned interatomic potential for the CrCoNi system within the neuroevolution potential (NEP) framework, achieving near first-principles accuracy with high computational efficiency. Trained on a comprehensive dataset spanning pure elements, binary and ternary alloys across a wide compositional range, diverse crystal structures and thermodynamic conditions, and based on spin-polarized \textit{ab initio} data, the model accurately reproduces equations of state, phonons, elastic constants, dislocation dissociation, surface and defect energies, melting temperatures and strain-induced phase transformations. It further captures SRO and its effect on stacking fault energies across both equimolar and non-equimolar compositions, in agreement with first-principles and experiments. In contrast to existing potentials, typically limited to equimolar alloys and less accurate for pure elements, the present model delivers consistent accuracy across the full compositional space while retaining superior efficiency. These results enable reliable atomistic simulations of composition-dependent behaviour and provide a framework for the design of non-equimolar CrCoNi alloys. 50. DeepFAN, a transformer-based deep learning model for human-artificial intelligence collaborative assessment of incidental pulmonary nodules in CT scans: a multi-reader, multi-case trial

  • 链接：https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.25607v1
  • 来源：arxiv
  • 摘要：The widespread adoption of CT has notably increased the number of detected lung nodules. However, current deep learning methods for classifying benign and malignant nodules often fail to comprehensively integrate global and local features, and most of them have not been validated through clinical trials. To address this, we developed DeepFAN, a transformer-based model trained on over 10K pathology-confirmed nodules and further conducted a multi-reader, multi-case clinical trial to evaluate its efficacy in assisting junior radiologists. DeepFAN achieved diagnostic area under the curve (AUC) of 0.939 (95% CI 0.930-0.948) on an internal test set and 0.954 (95% CI 0.934-0.973) on the clinical trial dataset involving 400 cases across three independent medical institutions. Explainability analysis indicated higher contributions from global than local features. Twelve readers' average performance significantly improved by 10.9% (95% CI 8.3%-13.5%) in AUC, 10.0% (95% CI 8.9%-11.1%) in accuracy, 7.6% (95% CI 6.1%-9.2%) in sensitivity, and 12.6% (95% CI 10.9%-14.3%) in specificity (P<0.001 for all). Nodule-level inter-reader diagnostic consistency improved from fair to moderate (overall k: 0
  • 易漏细节梳理：

当前的深度学习方法往往难以全面整合全局和局部特征，这导致了在结节分类任务上的性能受限。大多数用于结节分类的深度学习方法尚未经过临床验证。然而，DeepFAN在内部测试集上达到了0.939的诊断AUC，在临床试验数据集上更是达到了0.954的诊断AUC。解释性分析表明，全局特征对诊断结果有更高的贡献。在一项涉及12名读者的研究中，DeepFAN显著提高了他们的平均性能：AUC提高了10.9%，准确率提高了10.0%，敏感性提高了7.6%，特异性提高了12.6%。此外，结节水平的读者间诊断一致性从“中等”提升到了“良好”。这表明DeepFAN可能有助于不同机构之间的诊断质量标准化。该研究共涉及来自三个独立医疗机构的400个病例，并且临床试验已在中国临床试验注册中心注册。模型是在超过10,000个病理确认结节的数据集上进行训练的。因此，DeepFAN不仅提高了诊断性能，还可能在不同机构间实现诊断质量的标准化。

  • 关键点（易漏细节）：
  • current deep learning methods often fail to comprehensively integrate global and local features
  • most deep learning methods for nodule classification have not been clinically validated
  • DeepFAN achieved a diagnostic AUC of 0.939 on an internal test set
  • DeepFAN achieved a diagnostic AUC of 0.954 on a clinical trial dataset
  • explainability analysis indicated higher contributions from global features
  • twelve readers' average performance significantly improved by 10.9% in AUC
  • twelve readers' average performance significantly improved by 10.0% in accuracy
  • twelve readers' average performance significantly improved by 7.6% in sensitivity
  • twelve readers' average performance significantly improved by 12.6% in specificity
  • nodule-level inter-reader diagnostic consistency improved from fair to moderate
  • DeepFAN may help homogenize diagnostic quality across different institutions
  • the study involved 400 cases across three independent medical institutions
  • the clinical trial was registered with the Chinese Clinical Trial Registry
  • the model was trained on over 10,000 pathology-confirmed nodules

[2603.25607v1] DeepFAN, a transformer-based deep learning model for human-artificial intelligence collaborative assessment of incidental pulmonary nodules in CT scans: a multi-reader, multi-case trial Computer Science > Computer Vision and Pattern Recognition arXiv:2603.25607v1 (cs) [Submitted on 26 Mar 2026] Title: DeepFAN, a transformer-based deep learning model for human-artificial intelligence collaborative assessment of incidental pulmonary nodules in CT scans: a multi-reader, multi-case trial Authors: Zhenchen Zhu , Ge Hu , Weixiong Tan , Kai Gao , Chao Sun , Zhen Zhou , Kepei Xu , Wei Han , Meixia Shang , Xiaoming Qiu , Yiqing Tan , Jinhua Wang , Zhoumeng Ying , Li Peng , Wei Song , Lan Song , Zhengyu Jin , Nan Hong , Yizhou Yu View a PDF of the paper titled DeepFAN, a transformer-based deep learning model for human-artificial intelligence collaborative assessment of incidental pulmonary nodules in CT scans: a multi-reader, multi-case trial, by Zhenchen Zhu and 18 other authors View PDF Abstract: The widespread adoption of CT has notably increased the number of detected lung nodules. However, current deep learning methods for classifying benign and malignant nodules often fail to comprehensively integrate global and local features, and most of them have not been validated through clinical trials. To address this, we developed DeepFAN, a transformer-based model trained on over 10K pathology-confirmed nodules and further conducted a multi-reader, multi-case clinical trial to evaluate its efficacy in assisting junior radiologists. DeepFAN achieved diagnostic area under the curve (AUC) of 0.939 (95% CI 0.930-0.948) on an internal test set and 0.954 (95% CI 0.934-0.973) on the clinical trial dataset involving 400 cases across three independent medical institutions. Explainability analysis indicated higher contributions from global than local features. Twelve readers' average performance significantly improved by 10.9% (95% CI 8.3%-13.5%) in AUC, 10.0% (95% CI 8.9%-11.1%) in accuracy, 7.6% (95% CI 6.1%-9.2%) in sensitivity, and 12.6% (95% CI 10.9%-14.3%) in specificity (P<0.001 for all). Nodule-level inter-reader diagnostic consistency improved from fair to moderate (overall k: 0.313 vs. 0.421; P=0.019). In conclusion, DeepFAN effectively assisted junior radiologists and may help homogenize diagnostic quality and reduce unnecessary follow-up of indeterminate pulmonary nodules. Chinese Clinical Trial Registry: ChiCTR2400084624. 深度学习(Deep Learning) - 堆叠自动编码器(Stacked AutoEncoder) - 《Deeplearning Algorithms Tutorial（深度学习算法教程）》 - 书栈网 · BookStack × 思维导图备注 关闭 堆叠自动编码器(Stacked AutoEncoder) 来源:KeKe-Li 浏览 9132 扫码 2021-04-11 09:00:55 Deeplearning Algorithms tutorial 堆叠自动编码器(Stacked AutoEncoder) 应用示例 Deeplearning Algorithms tutorial 谷歌的人工智能位于全球前列，在图像识别、语音识别、无人驾驶等技术上都已经落地。而百度实质意义上扛起了国内的人工智能的大旗，覆盖无人驾驶、智能助手、图像识别等许多层面。苹果业已开始全面拥抱机器学习，新产品进军家庭智能音箱并打造工作站级别Mac。另外，腾讯的深度学习平台Mariana已支持了微信语音识别的语音输入法、语音开放平台、长按语音消息转文本等产品，在微信图像识别中开始应用。全球前十大科技公司全部发力人工智能理论研究和应用的实现，虽然入门艰难，但是一旦入门，高手也就在你的不远处！ AI的开发离不开算法那我们就接下来开始学习算法吧！ 堆叠自动编码器(Stacked AutoEncoder) 自从Hinton 2006年的工作之后，越来越多的研究者开始关注各种自编码器模型相应的堆叠模型。实际上，自编码器（Auto-Encoder）是一个较早的概念了，比如Hinton等人在1986, 1989年的工作。 自编码器可以理解为一个试图去还原其原始输入的系统。 图中，虚线蓝色框内就是一个自编码器模型，它由编码器（Encoder）和解码器（Decoder）两部分组成，本质上都是对输入信号做某种变换。 编码器将输入信号x变换成编码信号y，而解码器将编码y转换成输出信号 ，即 而自编码器的目的是，让输出尽可能复现输入x.但是，这样问题就来了,如果f和g都是恒等映射，那就是 ,实际上事实确实如此，但这样的变换就没有什么用了，所以我们需要对中间信号y（也叫作“编码”）做一定的约束，这样，系统往往能学出很有趣的编码变换f和编码y。 在这里需要强调一点，对于自编码器，往往并不关系输出是什么，因常我们只需要关心中间层的编码，或者是从输入到编码的映射。在我们强迫编码y和输入x不同的情况下，系统还能够去复原原始信号x，那么说明编码y已经承载了原始数据的所有信息，但以一种不同的形式！这就是特征提取。这个是通过自动学出来的，事实上，自动学习原始数据的特征表达也是神经网络和深度学习的核心目的之一。 自编码器与神经网络，其中神经网络就是在对原始信号逐层地做非线性变换： 该网络把输入层数据 转换到中间层（隐层） ，再转换到输出层 。图中的每个节点代表数据的一个维度（偏置项图中未标出）。每两层之间的变换都是“线性变化”+“非线性激活”，用公式表示即为。图中的每个节点代表数据的一个维度（偏置项图中未标出）。每两层之间的变换都是“线性变化”+“非线性激活”，用公式表示为: 神经网络通常可以用于分类，这样可以得道从输入层到输出层的变换函数。因此，我们需要定义一个目标函数来衡量当前的输出和真实结果的差异，利用该函数去逐步调整（如梯度下降）系统的参数 ，以使得整个网络尽可能去拟合训练数据。如果有正则约束的话，还同时要求模型尽量简单（以防止过拟合）。 但是自编码器怎么表示呢？ 自编码器试图复现其原始输入，因此，在训练中，网络中的输出应与输入相同，即 y=x，因此，一个自编码器的输入、输出应有相同的结构，即： 这里我们可以利用训练数据训练这个网络，等训练结束后，这个网络即学习出了 的能力。对我们来说，此时的h是至关重要的，因为它是在尽量不损失信息量的情况下，对原始数据的另一种表达。结合神经网络的惯例，我们再将自编码器的公式表示如下：（假设激活函数是sigmoid，用s表示） 其中， 表示损失函数，结合数据的不同形式，可以是二次误差（squared error loss）或交叉熵误差（cross entropy loss）。如果 ，一般称为tied weights。 这里我们会给隐层加入一定的约束。从数据维度来看，常见以下两种情况： n>p，即隐层维度小于输入数据维度。从x→h的变换是一种降维的操作，网络试图以更小的维度去描述原始数据而尽量不损失数据信息。实际上，当每两层之间的变换均为线性，且监督训练的误差是二次型误差时，该网络等价于PCA！ n<p ，即隐层维度大于输入数据维度。虽然我们同时约束h的表达尽量稀疏（有大量维度为0，未被激活），此时的编码器便是非常有名的“稀疏自编码器”。可为什么稀疏的表达就是好的？这是因为，有人尝试从人脑机理对比，人类神经系统在某一刺激下，大部分神经元是被抑制的。 学习过深度学习的都明白，深度学习中深度网络的重要性在于其能够逐层地学习原始数据的多种表达。每一层的都以底一层的表达为基础，但往往更抽象，更加适合复杂的分类等任务。 堆叠自编码器实际上就在做这样的事情，如前所述，单个自编码器通过虚构 的三层网络，能够学习出一种特征变化 (这里用θ表示变换的参数，包括W,b和激活函数)。实际上，当训练结束后，输出层就没什么意义了，我们一般会将其去掉的，即将自编码器表示为: 自编码器模型这里表示为3层的神经网络，这是因为训练的需要，我们将原始数据作为假想的目标输出，以此构建监督误差来训练整个网络。等训练结束后，输出层就可以去掉了，而我们关心的只是从x到h的变换过程。 接下来的思路就很自然了——我们已经得到特征表达h，那么我们就可以将h再当做原始信息，训练一个新的自编码器，得到新的特征表达。 堆叠自编码器（Stacked Auto-Encoder, SAE）,这里Stacked就是逐层垒叠的意思，跟“栈”有点像，当把多个自编码器Stack起来之后就是如下的过程： 这里需要注意的是，整个网络的训练不是一蹴而就的，而是需要逐层进行。根据n,m,k结构，实际上我们是先训练网络n→m→n，得到n→m的变换，然后再训练 m→k→m，得到m→k的变换。最终堆叠成SAE，即为n→m→k的结果，整个过程就像一层层往上构建网络，这个就是非常有名的 layer-wise unsuperwised pre-training（逐层非监督预训练）。 稀疏自编码器如前所示，这种模型背后的思想是，高维而稀疏的表达是好的。一般而言h中哪些节点是被抑制的（对于sigmoid单元即输出为0），而是指定一个稀疏性参数ρ，，代表隐藏神经元的平均活跃程度（在训练集上取平均）。比如，当ρ=0.05时，可以认为隐层节点在95%的时间里都是被一直的，只有5%的机会被激活。实际上，为了满足这一条件，隐层神经元的活跃度需要接近于0。 既然要求平均激活度为ρ，那么我们只要引入一个度量，来衡量神经元i的实际激活度 与期望激活度ρ之间的差异即可，然后将这个度量添加到目标函数作为正则，训练整个网络即可。那么，什么样的度量适合这个任务呢？了解过概率论、信息论基础的人应该清楚——相对熵，也就是KL散度（KL divergence）。因此，整个网络所添加的惩罚项： 我们可以从下图（摘自UFLDL）中直观理解KL散度作为惩罚项的含义。图中假设平均激活度ρ=0.2。 可以看出，当 一旦偏离期望激活度ρ，这种误差便急剧增大，从而作为惩罚项添加到目标函数，指导整个网络学习出稀疏的特征表达。 降噪自编码器(Stacked Denoising Autoencoders)核心思想是，一个能够从中恢复出原始信号的表达未必是最好的，能够对“被污染/破坏”的原始数据编码、解码，然后还能恢复真正的原始数据，这样的特征才是好的。 假设原始数据x被我们“故意破坏”，比如加入高斯白噪，或者把某些维度数据抹掉，变成了 ，然后再对 编码、解码，得到恢复信号 ，该恢复信号尽可能逼近未被污染的数据x。此时，监督训练的误差从 变成了 。 降噪自编码器的系统结构如下图: 深度学习兴起正式因为逐层预训练方法的提出，使得深度网络的训练成为可能。对于一个深度网络而言，这种逐层预训练的方法，正是前面介绍的这种堆叠自动编码器(Stacked AutoEncoder)。对于常见的分类任务，一般分为以下两个阶段： 逐层预训练(layer-wise pre-training) 微调(fune-tuning ) 上面讲述的的自动编码器，本质上都是非监督学习，自动编码器各层的输出都是原始数据的不同表达。对于分类任务，往往在自动编码器顶端再添加一分类层（如Softmax层），并结合有标注的训练数据，在误差函数的指导下，对系统的参数进行微调，以使得整个网络能够完成所需的分类任务。 对于微调过程，即可以只调整分类层的参数（此时相当于把整个SAE当做一个feature extractor），也可以调整整个网络的参数（适合训练数据量比较大的情况）。 但是为什么训练稀疏自编码器为什么一般都是三层的结构，实际上这里的三层是指训练单个自编码器所假想的3层神经网络，这对任何基于神经网络的编码器都是这样。多层的稀疏自编码器自然是有的，只不过是通过layer-wise pre-training这种方式逐层堆叠起来的，而不是直接去训练多层的网络。 实际上，这正是在训练深层神经网络中遇到的问题。直接去训练一个深层的自编码器，其实本质上就是在做深度网络的训练，由于梯度扩散等问题，这样的网络往往根本无法训练。这倒不是因为会破坏稀疏性等原因，只要网络能够训练，对模型施加的约束总能得到相应的结果。 但是为什么逐层预训练就可以使得深度网络的训练成为可能了呢？其实一个直观的解释是，预训练好的网络在一定程度上拟合了训练数据的结构，这使得整个网络的初始值是在一个合适的状态，便于有监督阶段加快迭代收敛。 应用示例 当前内容版权归 KeKe-Li 或其关联方所有，如需对内容或内容相关联开源项目进行关注与资助，请访问 KeKe-Li . 上一篇: 下一篇: Deeplearning Algorithms
